   <h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading">GNOME Desktop icons</h1> 
   <div id="bodyContent" class="vector-body"> 
    <div id="siteSub" class="noprint">
     From Wikimedia Commons, the free media repository
    </div> 
    <div id="contentSub"></div> 
    <div id="contentSub2"></div> 
    <div id="jump-to-nav"></div> <a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a> <a class="mw-jump-link" href="#searchInput">Jump to search</a> 
    <div id="mw-content-text" class="mw-body-content mw-content-ltr" lang="en" dir="ltr">
     <div class="mw-parser-output">
      <p><b>This contains GNOME Desktop Tango icons.</b> For the original Tango icons see: <i><b><a href="/wiki/Tango_icons" title="Tango icons">Tango icons</a></b></i>. <i>See also <a href="/wiki/GNOME_High_contrast_icons" title="GNOME High contrast icons">GNOME High contrast icons</a></i>. </p>
      <p>GNOME Desktop icons contains the default icon theme used by the GNOME desktop. The icons are used in the panel menu, and in nautilus and other applications, to represent the different applications, files, directories, and devices. Below are all unique icons from <b>gnome-icon-theme 2.20.0</b>. All icons are licensed under GNU General Public License version 2. </p> 
      <style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r565310027">@media all and (max-width:720px){.mw-parser-output .tocright{display:none}}.mw-parser-output .tocright{float:right;clear:right;width:auto;background:none;padding:.5em 0 .8em 1.4em;margin-bottom:.5em}.mw-parser-output .tocright-clear-left{clear:left}.mw-parser-output .tocright-clear-both{clear:both}.mw-parser-output .tocright-clear-none{clear:none}</style>

      <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="View">View</span></h4> 
      <ul class="gallery mw-gallery-nolines"> 
       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 53px">
        <div style="width: 53px">

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Emotes">Emotes</span></h2> 
      <div style="text-align:right; line-height:.8; font-size:85%; margin:-1.5em 0 0 2em; font-style:italic;">
       <sup>Transcluded from <a href="/wiki/GNOME_Desktop_icons,_emotes" title="GNOME Desktop icons, emotes">GNOME Desktop icons, emotes</a></sup>
      </div> 
      <ul class="gallery mw-gallery-nolines"> 
       <li class="gallerycaption"><a href="/wiki/Category:GNOME_Desktop_icons,_SVG_emotes" title="Category:GNOME Desktop icons, SVG emotes">Scalable release</a> 2.20.0</li> 
       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 53px">
        <div style="width: 53px">

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Places">Places</span></h2> 
      <ul class="gallery mw-gallery-nolines"> 
       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 53px">
        <div style="width: 53px">
